\begin{entry}
\word{aikayxsathxla}
\meaning{\arthanonum{Bakatx, maheVsha, parxsAdi, pArxNaliMgi, sharaNa matutx aikayx eMba SaTfsathxlagaLalilx koneya sathxla. aMga enisikoMDiruva jiVvanu liMga eMdu kareyalAguva shivanoMdige samarasa\-vanunx nirUpisuva sathxla.}}
\smallskip
\begin{shl}
Adw BakatxsathxlaM porxVkatxM tatoV mAheVshavxrasathxlamf |\\[1pt]
parxsAdisathxlamanayxtutx pArxNaliMgisathxlaM tataH |\\[1pt]
sharaNasathxlamAKAyxtaM SaSaThxmeYkayxsathxlaM matamf ||
\end{shl}
\medskip
\pauthor{(si.shi., 5. 24)}
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{aikayxsathxlakekx saMbaMdhisida nAlukx aMgasathxlagaLalilx oMdu. iMdirxya viSayagaLiMda
uMTAguva AnaMdadalilx nisapxqqha\-nAgi nimaRlacitatxnAda sAdhakanu shivAnaMdaveMba
mahAsamudarxdalilx muLuguva aikayxna savxrUpavanunx nirUpisuva aikayxsathxlaveMba
avAMtarasathxla. ANavAdi malagaLa saMpakaR\-vanunx kaLedukoMDa, niSakxLaMkavAda
manoVvAyxpAravuLaLx sAdha\-kanu shivoV{\char'263}haMBAvadalilx sadA maganxnAda shivayoVgiyu
shiveYkayxteyanunx hoMdutAtxne.}}
\smallskip
\begin{shl}
aikayxsathxlamidaM porxVkatxM catudhAR munipuMgava |\\[1pt]
\qquad\qquad aikayxmAcArasaMpatitxH... ||\\[1pt]
viSayAnaMdakaNikA niHsapxqqhoV nimaRlAshayaH |\\[1pt]
shivAnaMdamahAsiMdhumajajxnAdeYkayxmucayxteV ||\\[1pt]
nidhURtamalasaMbaMdhoV niSakxlaMkamanoVgataH |\\[1pt]
shivoV{\char'263}hamiti BAveVna nirUDhoV hi shiveYkayxtAmf ||
\end{shl}
\medskip
\pauthor{(si.shi., 14, 3-5)}
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{aikayxsathxlada BeVda - aikayxsathxla, AcArasaMpatitxsathxla, EkaBAjanasathxla matutx
sahaBoVjanasathxlaveMdu aikayxsathxlAMtagaRta aMgasathxlagaLu nAlukx. sivxVkaqtaparxsAdi,
shiSoTxVdana, carAcaralaya, BAMDa, BAjana, aMgAleVpa, savxparAjacnx, BAvABAvavinAsha matutx
jAcnxnashUnayx eMdu liMgasathxlagaLu oMbatutx.}}
\smallskip
\begin{shl}
aikayxsathxlamidaM porxVkatxM catudhAR munipuMgava |\\[1pt]
aikayxmAcArasaMpatitxH EkaBAjanameVva ca |\\[1pt]
sahaBoVjanamiteyxVSAM... ||
\end{shl}
\smallskip
\pauthor{(si.shi., 14. 3)}
\medskip
\begin{shl}
sathxlAnAM navakaM ceYkayxsathxleV{\char'263}simxnf parikiVtayxRteV |\\[1pt]
tatfsivxVkaqtaparxsAdeYkayxsathxlamAdw parxkiVtiRtamf ||\\[1pt]
shiSoTxVdanasathxlaM cAtha carAcaralayasathxlamf ||\\[1pt]
BAMDasathxlaM tataH porxVkatxM BAjanasathxlamutatxmamf ||\\[1pt]
aMgAleVpasathxlaM pashAcxtf savxparAjacnxsathxlaM tataH ||\\[1pt]
BAvABAvavinAshaM ca jAcnxnashUnayxsathxlaM tataH |
\end{shl}
\medskip
\pauthor{(si.shi., 20. 2-5)}
%\newmeaning{\arthanonum{AdhAyxtimxka jiVvanada Aru meTiTxlugaLalilx koneyadu. idanunx talupidavanu jiVvanada paramadheyxVyavAda liMgAMga sAmarasayxvanunx sAdhisutAtxne. (noVDi : {\bf aikayx, Bakitx})}}
% \newmeaning{\arthanonum{moVkaSxsAdhaneya Aru haMtagaLeMdu parigaNisiruva Bakatx, mAheVshavxra, parxsAdi, pArxNaliMgi, sharaNa matutx aikayx- eMba Aru sathxlagaLalilx koneyasathxla;}}
\newmeaning{\ullekha{biVjavaqkaSx yoVgadaMte Bakatxsathxla shiKikapuRra yoVgadaMte aikayxsathxla (savasaM. 6; Adayayx. 1039-329); paramAnaMdarUpanAda sharaNaM tAneMba\char'273\char'236vaM {ma\char'273\char'304\char'311dada\char'273} samxraNedoV\char'273de mahAliMgeYkayxvaneYdida BeVda\-veMtidiRtetxMdoDe muMde aikayxsathxlavAdudu (keYvasha. 71-1 sUtarx).}}
\newmeaning{\ni{aikayxsathxlaM - aikayxsayx sathxlaM  aikayxsathxlaM; aikayxM iti sathxlaM  aikayxsathxlaM}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{aikayxsathxla tirxvidha}
\src{va}
\meaning{\arthanonum{kAyaliMgeYkayx, jiVvaliMgeYkayx matutx BAva\-liMgeYkayx; - eMbudAgi aikayxsathxladalilx mUru viBAgagaLu:} \ullekha{aikayxsathxlatirxvidha, kAyaliMgeYkayx, jiVvaliMgeYkayx, BAvaliMgeYkayx: adakekx vivara: kirxyeya\char'273tude kAyaliMgeYkayx. anuBAvavaratude jiVva\-liMgeYkayx. a\char'273\char'236vu sine baMjeyAdude BAvaliMgeYkayx. (savasaM. 3; cenanxba. 987-322).}}
\end{entry}

%\begin{entry}
%\word{aikayxsathxla tirxvidha}
%\meaning{\arthanonum{saMpUNaR sharaNAdavanige tAnu eMba ahaMBAvavilalx. tAnu
% savxtaMtarx hAgU parxteyxVka vayxkitxyalalxveMdU tAnu

% parashivanoMdige aikayxvAguvudu sAdhayxvilalx. parashivanoMdige
% aikayxteyanunx sAdhisidavanu aikayxsathxladalilxdAdxne eMdathaR.}}
%\newmeaning{\arthanonum{aikayxsathxladalilxyU mUru upasathxlagaLive. aveMdare: kAya
% liMgeYkayx, jiVvaliMgeYkayx, BAvaliMgeYkayx. kAyaliMgeYkayxna
% parxtiyoMdu kAyakavU deYviVkAyaRdaMte irutatxdeyeV horatu
% sAvxthaRbudidhxya mAnavakAyakadaMtiruvudilalx. avanu tananx
% liMgeYkayxBAvavanunx nisAvxthaR kAyakada mUlaka toVrisidAga, avana
% kAya liMgeYkayx enisikoLuLxtAtxne. tAnu parashivanalilx oMdaMshaveV
% horatu, tAnu parxteyxVka vayxkitxyalalx eMba BAvavu avana

\begin{entry}
\word{aikayxsathxlaparavasutxBAvanAshana}
\src{va}
\meaning{\arthanonum{sAdhakanu tananx AdhAyxtimxka sAdhaneya vividha haMtagaLalilx
 tAnu matutx parashiva beVre beVre eMdu tiLidu avananunx
 pUjisutAtxne, avanige tananxnunx apiRsikoLuLxtAtxne. Adare
 aikayxsathxladalilx jAcnxtaq-jecnxVyagaLa BeVdavilalxdaMte avanu
 shivanalilx oMdAdAga, tAnu sAdhakaneMba BAvavU
 nAshavAgutatxdeyalalxde, parashiva pUjayxneMba BAvavU
 nAshavAgutatxde. shiva beVre eMba BAva hoVgadidadxre, avanu
 aikayxsathxlavanunx sAdhisilalxveMdathaR. (va.pa.koV. 103)} \ullekha{Bakatxsathxla barxhamxnAshana, mAheVshavxrasathxla viSuNxnAshana, parxsAdisathxla rudarxnAshana, pArxNaliMgisathxla IshavxranAshana, sharaNasathxla sadAshivanAshana, aikayxsathxla paramavasutx BAvanAshana. (savasaM. 8; moVLige. 2005-649).}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{aidaMga}
\src{va}
\meaning{\arthanonum{parashivana aidu aMgagaLu. aveMdare : satutx, citutx, AnaMda, nitayx, paripUNaR. vAsatxvavAgi ililx `aMga' eMba padavu BAga athavA deVha eMbathaRdalilx baLakeyAgirade, guNa athavA aMsha eMbathaRdalilx baLakeyAgide. shUnayxsithxtiyalilxruvAga parashivanige I yAva guNavU iralilalx. Adare, parashiva\-nige tAnobabxneV iruvudara arivuMTAgutatxde.}
\ullekha{satutxcitAtxnaMda nitayxparipUNaRveMba aidaMgava gaBiRVkarisikoMDu nitayxnijadAraMBakekx hoVgi paravashavAda soVjigava noVDA (savasaM. 10; jakakxNa. 1582-691); aidaMgadaMganeyAnu bArayAyx aidu keLadiyarenage noVDayAyx, hiriya kAlada deVvara varavenagayAyx, beVDidudx mADi mane tuMbisuva bArayAyx (savasaM. 12; deVshikeVM. 175-52).}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{aidara guNa}
\src{va}
\meaning{\arthanonum{paMcaBUtagaLa guNa. parxtiyoMdu BUtadalilx aidU BUtagaLa
 guNagaLidadxrU, oMdoMdakUkx tananxdeV Ada vishiSaTx
 guNavirutatxde. udAharaNege paqthivxVtatatxvXvu kaThiNateya saMkeVta;
 adakekx gaMdhaveV vishiSaTx guNa. hiVge niVrige rasa, aginxge rUpa, vAyuvige
 sapxshaR hAgU AkAshakekx shabadx ivu vishiSaTx
 guNagaLu. ivugaLanunx parxteyxVkavAgi apiRsi \hbox{mukitx} paDeyutetxVneMdu
yArAdarU heVLidare adu keVvala suLaLxlalx, asAdhayxda mAtU
hwdu. EkeMdare paMcaBUtagaLanAnxgali, avugaLa vishiSaTx
guNagaLanAnxgali parxteyxVkavAgi noVDalu sAdhayxvilalx.} \ullekha{aidara guNavaDagi, mUrara guNa mugidu, Arara guNa hAri, eMTara guNada neMTatanava baMdhisi toVrutatxdakekx munanxve mana jAri niMditu. (savasaM. 8; moVLige. 1917-646).}}

\begin{entry}
\word{aidu iMdirxyagaLa cakarx}
\src{va}
\meaning{\arthanonum{kelavu dashaRnagaLa parxkAra kelavu pArxNigaLige oMdiMdirxya,
 kelavakekx eraDu, kelavakekx mUru, kelavakekx nAlukx iMdirxyagaLu
 irutatxve. manuSayxnige aidU iMdirxyagaLive. vacanakArara parxkAra
 Bavavu oMdu cakarx. cakarxkekx AdiyAgali, aMtayxvAgali
 ilalx. hAgeyeV saqSiTxya oMdu BAgavAgiruva manuSayxnu cakarxda
 kaDiDxgaLaMte aneVka bAri saqSiTxyAgidAdxne; hAgU tananx kamaRkekx
 takakxMte matetx saqSiTxyAgutAtxne. Aga avana iMdirxyagaLAda kaNuNx,
kivi, mUgu, camaR matutx nAlagegaLU avanalilx utapxtitxyAgutatxve. I
aidu iMdirxyagaLa cakarxgaLu tirugadidadxre (vAyxpAragaLu
naDeyadidadxre), aMdare, manuSayx yAvudeV riVtiya kamaRgaLanunx
mADadidadxre, Aga avanige
pApapuNayxgaLuMTAguvudilalx. pApapuNayxgaLuMTAgadidadxre
saqSiTxyAguvudilalx. AdudariMda rUpacakarx (nayanacakarx) itAyxdigaLa
cakarxgaLu tirugadidadxre, loVkAdiloVkagaLeV iruvudilalx. (va.pa.koV. 104)} \ullekha{rUpa cakarx nayanadiMde naDevudu; shabadx cakarx shoVtarxdiMde naDevudu, swraBacakarx GArxNadiMde naDevudu, rucicakarx jihevxyiMde naDevudu, sapxshaRcakarx tavxkikxniMde naDevudu loVkAdiloVkaMgaLelalx (savasaM. 3; cenanxba. 1501-549).}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{aivatatxkaSxra}
\src{va}
\meaning{\arthanonum{mAnavana deVhadalilx Aru
 cakarxgaLive eMdu naMbalAgutatxde. I cakarxgaLige padamxgaLeMdU
 kareyalAgidudx, parxtiyoMdu padamxkUkx tananxdeV Ada vishiSaTx
 saMKeyxya esaLu (daLa) gaLiveyeMdU, A esaLugaLa meVle
 akaSxragaLiveyeMdU naMbalAgutatxde. avugaLa vivara I parxkAra
 ide:}}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{AdhAra athavA mUlAdhAra padamxdalilx nAlukx daLagaLive. avugaLa
 meVle va, sha, Sa matutx sa eMba nAlukx akaSxragaLive. adakikxMta
 meVliruva sAvxdhiSAThxna padamxdalilx Aru daLagaLidudx, avugaLa
 meVle ba, Ba, ma, ya, ra matutx la eMba Aru akaSxragaLanunx
 bareyalAgide. adakikxMta meVliruva maNipUraka cakarxkekx hatutx
 daLagaLidudx, avugaLa meVle Da, Dha, Na, ta, tha, da, dha, na, pa
 matutx Pa eMba hatutx akaSxragaLu mUDive. adakikxMta inUnx meVliruva
anAhata padamxdalilx hanenxraDu daLagaLidudx avugaLa meVle ka, Ka, ga,
Ga, kna, ca, Ca, ja, jha, cna, Ta matutx Tha eMba hanenxraDu
akaSxragaLu mUDive. anAhata padamxda meVliruva vishudidhx padamxdalilx
hadinAru esaLugaLidudx, avugaLa meVle, a, A, i, I, u, U, Qu, QU, laq,
lUq, E, ai, O, au, aM, aH eMba hadinAru akaSxragaLu mUDive. I aidU
cakarxgaLu manuSayxna meVrudaMDadalilx (benunxhuri\-yoLage) ive eMdu

eraDakaSxragaLu mUDirutatxve eMdU naMba\-lAgide.}}

\begin{entry}
\word{oMdiMdirxya modalAgi aidiMdirxya kaDeyAda pArxNigaLu}
\src{va}
\meaning{\arthanonum{jeYnara parxkAra, iMdirxyagaLa saMKeyxya AdhArada meVle
 pArxNigaLanunx vagiVRkarisalAgidudx, vacanakAraru A tatatxvXvanunx
 opipxkoMDaMte kANutatxde. I tatatxvXda parxkAra, pArxNigaLanunx hiVge
 vagiVRkarisalAgide :}}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\artha{oMdeV iMdirxyavanunxLaLx pArxNigaLu : EkANu jiVvigaLige 
 keVvala sapxshaRneVMdirxyavoMdeV idudx, uLida yAva
 iMdirxyagaLilalx.}}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\artha{huLagaLu, shaMKada huLa, jigaNe muMtAda pArxNigaLige
 sapxshaRneVMdirxya matutx GArxNeVMdirxya eMba eraDeV
 iMdirxyagaLirutatxve.}}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\artha{tigaNe, heVnu, iruve, diVpada huLagaLu, muMtAda pArxNigaLige
 sapxshaRneVMdirxya, GArxNeVMdirxya matutx nayaneVMdirxya eMba mUru
 mAtarx iMdirxyagaLirutatxve.}}
\newmeaning{\artha{jeVnuhuLa, noNa, soLeLx muMtAda jiVvigaLige GArxNeVMdirxya,
 nayaneVMdirxya, shorxVterxVMdirxya matutx rasaneVMdirxya eMba nAlukx
iMdirxyagaLidudx adakekx tavxgiMdirxya (sapxshaRneVMdirxya)
iruvudilalx.}}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\artha{miVnu, mosaLe, hasugaLaMtha catuSApxdi, hakikx, koVti,
 manuSayx I elalx pArxNigaLige meVle heVLida aidU
 iMdirxyagaLirutatxve. kaDime iMdirxyagaLiruvudu pArxNivagaRda keLa 
 aMtasatxnunx toVrisidare, hecucx iMdirxyagaLiruvudu pArxNigaLu
 hecucx vikAsavAgiruvudara doyxVtakavAgide.}}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\artha{ililx atayxMta hecucx saMKeyxya iMdirxyagaLanunxLaLx mAnava\-nige
 budidhxyU hecicxruvudariMda, avanige mAtarx unanxta dheyxVyagaLa
 parxjecnxyirutatxde eMbudu gamanAhaR. (va.pa.koV. 105)}}
\newmeaning{\ullekha{mara giDa baLiLx dhAnayxMgaLa beLaselalxva taritaridu pArxNava\-koMduMDu, shariVrava horeva doVSakekx inAnxvudu vidhi\-yayAyx, oMdiMdirxya modalAgi aidiMdirxya kaDeyAda jiVva jAladalilxde carAcaravelalx. (savasaM. 1; basava. 1308-360)}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}

\meaning{\arthanonum{(= kaMthA = kaMthe = kaMte)}}
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{liMgagaLigU, basavana vigarxhagaLigU leVpisuvudakAkxgi tayArisida geVreNeNx hAgU kADigeya (kapURrada hoge/diVpada hoge) \hbox{kariya} misharxNa:}
\ullekha{bUdi kaMtiya baDidu rananxkaMteya tiVDi joVgirUpavu opupxvado deVvA (kananxjA. 349-26).}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}

deMtu baNiNxsalApaRnAM KagakoVTi rucimayava
\end{shl}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\ullekha{kaMtuhara aBayakara, enanx neVmakekx aDaDx barutitxradiru. oDave savedaroDalanoDuDxve. kaDaguvaDomemx haLaci noVDu. (savasaM. 9; suMkabaM. 710-216); A parashivana aSATxMgadiMdAda barxhAmxMDada sithxra cara pArxNigaLa layava noVDi ciMteyoLagAgi, kaMtuharana dhAyxnava mADalu, A hara gururUpava tALudx baMdu, tananx ciMtisida sujAcnxnigaLige, manavanobubxLigoLisuvudakekx kAraNaveMdu heVLida. (savasaM. 13; maDivA. 983-445); kaMtuharanipapx sejejxya sobaganoLagoMDu \hbox{eseva} puradoLagelalx haramayaM shivamayaM [tirura. 2-14].}}
\end{entry}

\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\qquad shivaliMga athavA adara parxkAshavAda aGoVramuKa (mUtiRsAdAKayx) vanunx aMtashacxkuSxviniMda noVDabeVkenunxva sAdhakanu vidAyxkaleyanunx olisikoLuLxva parxyatanx mADutAtxne. vidAyxkaleyanunx sAdhisidavanu rudArxkiSx, viBUti matutx liMgavanunx dharisutAtxnalalxde beVrAva AlaMkArika vasutxgaLanUnx dharisuvudilalx, shivaliMgavanunx noVDutAtxnalalxde yAva moVhaka vasutx\-vanUnx noVDuvudilalx; parxsAdavananxlalxde EnanUnx tinunxvudilalx. \meaning{\arthanonum{liMgAMga sAmarasayxda naMtara sAdhakana kAyadalilx aneVka badalAvaNe uMTAgutatxde. kAyada bayakegaLu kaDimeyAgutatxdeyalalxde, tananx kAyavu tananxdalalx adu shivanadeMdu parigaNisutAtxne. hiVge tAnu kAyavanunx kaLedukoMDu adanunx shivanalilx kANuvudeV `kAya akAyadalilx aDaguvudu' eninxsikoLuLxtatxde.}
\ullekha{kAya akAyadalilx aDagi, jiVva nijiVRvadalilx aDagi, Barxme saMcAra\-vilalxde, mahAGanadalilx saMdu, uBayada saMdilalxde baMkeVshavxra liMgadalilx sale saMdavana olume (savasaM. 9; suMkabaM. 635-199).}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{kAyaka}
\src{va}
\meaning{\arthanonum{samapaRNaBAvadiMda mADuva kelasa; shivA\-paRNegAgiyeV mADuva kAyaR.}
\ullekha{deVvasahita Bakatx manege baMdaDe kAyakavAvudeMdu besagoMDenAdaDe nimAmxNe! (savasaM. 1; basava. 453-109); kAya kAyakava mADutitxralu manavu liMgadalilx berasi terahilalxdipapx maDivALana pariya noVDA! (savasaM. 3; cenanxba. 845-251); kAyakadalilx niratanAdaDe, gurudashaRnavAdaDU mareyabeVku, liMgapUje\-yAdaDU mareyabeVku ...kAyakave keYlAsavAda kAraNa (savasaM. 6; Ayadxkikx. 1170-369).}
\arthanonum{kAyaka eMdare. yAvudeV vaqtitx athavA udoyxVga. Adare vacanakArara daqSiTxyalilx kAyakakekx vishiSaTx athaRvide. \hbox{adanunx} sUthxlavAgi vivarisabahudu.}}
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{satayxshudadhx kAyakavaSeTxV kAyaka. hiMse, vaMcane, suLuLx muMtAda aneYtika kAyakavu kAyakavenisikoLuLxvudilalx. kAyava baLalisade sumamxne kuLitu uNuNxvudu kAyaka tatatxvXkekx
 virudadhx. aMdare elalxrU kAyaka mADaleVbeVku. kAyava
 savesaleVbeVku. `kAyava baLa\-lisade, tanu karagade, mana noVyade,
 kADi beVDi' taruvudu kAyakavalalx. BikeSx mADuvudu, kaLaLxtana
 athavA moVsadiMda gaLisuvudu, adariMda baMdudanunx dAsoVha mADuvudu
 viVrasheYva sidAdhxMtakekx virudadhx.}}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{satayxshudadhx kAyakavu durAseyiMda kUDirabAradu. nALegoVsakxra
 duDiyuvudu, makakxLu momamxkakxLigoVsakxra uLisuvudu, aSeTxVke,
 iMdina agatayxkikxMta hecucx duDiyuvudu, kAyaka sidAdhxMtakekx
 horagu. vayxkitx tananx kuTuMbakekx aMdaMdige agatayxvAdaSaTxnunx
 mAtarx duDidare sAku. inUnx uLidudanunx jaMgamakekx
 niVDabeVku. hiVge elalxrU duDidare yArU parAva\-laMbigaLAgabeVkAgilalx, yArU BikuSxkarAgabeVkilalx.}
``beVDalAgadu Bakatx''. \arthanonum{hiVge iDiV samAjavu samaqdidhxyiMda tuMbi
 tuLukutitxrutatxde} ``citatxshudadhx kAyaka mADuva sadaBxkatxna
 maneyalilx etatx noVDidaDatatx lakiSxmX tAneV
 tAnAgipapxLu''. \arthanonum{agatayxkikxMta hecucx duDidare, kAyava baLalisade
 vaMcane, suLuLx, kaLaLxtana muMtAda aneYtika riVtiyalilx duDidare,
 manuSayxnu Alasi, duvayxRsani, durAcAri, adhamiRyAgutAtxne. duSaTx 
 kAyaka mADi liMgAMgasAmarasayx sAdhisalu
 sAdhayxvilalx. satAkxyakadiMda samAjada AthiRka
 parxgatiyAguvudaSeTx alalx, samAjadalilx shAMti, samAdhAnagaLU uMTAgutatxve. nALe\-geMtoV eMba ciMteyanunx dUramADi namamx AhAra\-vanunx nALe yArU doVcikoMDu hoVguvudilalx eMba samAdhAnavanunx mUDisuvudeV kAyakada udedxVsha.}}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{kAyakavu sharaNara daqSiTxyalilx keVvala veYyakitxka athavA kwTuM\-bika vaqtitxyAgirade, oMdu samAjaseVveyU Agitutx. aMtaha samAjaseVveyeMba kAyakagaLanunx sAmAnayxvAgi jaMgamaru mADutitxdadxru. avugaLalilx muKayxvAda kelavanunx ililx hesarisabahudu:}}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\artha{GaMTeya kAyaka : maThadalilxruva jaMgamaru parxtidina \hbox{beLagegx} nasukinalilx GaMTe bArisi, janaranunx ecacxragoLisutAtxre. nidedxyiMda janaru deYnaMdina kAyaRkarxmagaLanunx mugisi tamamx kAyakadalilx toDagali eMbudeV avaru GaMTe bArisuva udedxVsha.}}
\newmeaning{\artha{jaMgina kAyaka : maThadiMda sUyoVRdayakekx horabidadx
 jaMgamaru parxti Bakatxra maneyanunx parxveVshisi, malagiruvavaranunx
tamamx betatxdiMda tividu ecacxrisutAtxre. ivaru tamamx eDageYge jaMgu
(jaMgf jaMgf eMdu shababx mADuva GaMTe) kaTiTxkoMDu aDADxDuvudariMda
inUnx malagidadx \hbox{janaru} adara shabadxdiMda edudx, muKamAjaRne
itAyxdigaLalilx niratarAgutAtxre. ivaru maneyoLage baMdu
ebibxsidudakAkxgi janaru avarige BikeSx niVDutAtxre. AdudariMda
avarige jaMgina ayayx eMba hesarU ide.}}
\newmeaning{\artha{hiTiTxna kAyaka : sumAru 9 athavA 10 gaMTege (beLagina hotutx) hiTiTxna ayayxnavaru Bakatxra manege baMdu janaru sAnxna\-pUjAdi\-gaLalilx niratarAgidAdxroV ilalxvoV, tamamx kAyakagaLalilx niratarAgidAdxro athavA \hbox{inUnx} malagidAdxroV eMdu pariVkiSx\-sutAtxre. avaru mADida seVvege parxtiPalaveMbaMte Bakatxru avarige oMdu hiDi hiTaTxnunx niVDutAtxre. avarige hiTiTxna ayayxnavareMdu hesaru. hiVge Bakatxra veYyakitxka, kwTuMbika matutx sAmAjika naDenuDiyanunx rUpisuva saluvAgi jaMgamaru meVlina nayavAda riVtigaLanunx anusarisutAtxre. Adare idAvudakUkx bagagxda kela janarirutAtxre; avaranunx tidadxlAgadavareMdu jaMgamaru hAgeV biTuTxbiDuvudilalx. aMthavaranunx tididx dhAmiRka hAdige tarabeVkeMba udedxVshadiMda avaru tekekxya kAyaka, muLALxvigeya kAyaka matutx shasatxrXda kAyaka eMba mUru kAyakagaLanunx mADutAtxre.}}
\newmeaning{\artha{tekekxya kAyaka : GaMTeya kAyaka, jaMgina kAyaka matutx hiTiTxna kAyakadayayxgaLu oMdeV Uralilx nelesida jaMgamarAdare,  tekekxya kAyakadayayxgaLu UrUru tiruguva jaMgamaru. avaru  maThadalilx vAsatxvayx hUDi, alilxna jaMgamariMda adhamiRgaLa paTiTx paDeyutAtxre. anaMtara A adhamiRya maneya muMde sUyoVRdayakikxMta  modaleV hoVgi niMtirutAtxre. bAgilu tegeda kUDaleV oLanugigx maneyalilxruva kaMbavanunx apipxkoLuLxtAtxre. A adhamiRyu tananx guruhiriyara kaSxme keVLabeVku, tAnu adhamaRvanunx tayxjisi dhamaRda hAdi hiDiyutetxVneMdu sAvxmigaLige vacana niVDuvavaregU avaru tamamx apupxgeyanunx saDilisuvudilalx. aMdare, alilxyavaregU avarige sAnxnavilalx, pUjeyilalx, parxsAdavilalx. idu oMdu dinavAgabahudu, eraDu athavA mUru dinagaLAgabahudu. oMdu veVLe adhamiRyu idakekx bagagxdidadxre sAvxmigaLu alelxV pArxNatAyxga mADabahudu. anaMtara adha\-miRge pashAcxtAtxpavAdarU Agabahudu.}}
\newmeaning{\artha{muLALxvige kAyaka : tekekxya kAyakadayayxgaLu adha\-miRya maneya oLage hoVgi tamamx kAyaka mADidare, muLALxvige kAyakadayayxgaLu tamamx kAyakavanunx A adhamiRya maneya muMde, rasetxyalilx niMtu mADuvaru. ivarU saha maThadalilx vAsatxvayx hUDi viSayalaMpaTara paTiTxyanunx paDedu mAraneya dinaveV tamamx kAyakavanunx pArxraMBisutAtxre. tekekxya kAyakadayayxgaLu hoVdareMba samAdhAnada meVle adhamiRyu tananx adhamaRvanunx matetx muMduvaresabahudu. aMtahavana maneya muMde sUyoVRdayada hotitxge muLALxvige kAyakadayayxgaLu, cUpAda moLegaLanunx joVDisida halageya meVle hAvugeya meVle aMgAlanunx Uri nilulxtAtxre. adhamiRya hesaranunx GaTiTxyAgi heVLutAtx, basavAdi sharaNara hesarugaLanunx samxrisutAtx, adhamiRge sadubxdidhxyanunx koDaleMdu shiva\-nanunx samxrisutAtx niMtare, Urina janarelalx adhamiRyanunx bayayxtoDagutAtxre. A avamAna sAladeMbaMte, tananx tapipxgAgi sAvxmigaLige noVvAgutitxde eMba pashAcxtAtxpavU avanalilx uMTAgi, avanu tananx tapapxnunx opipxkoMDu, inunx muMde dhAmiRka jiVvana naDesuvudAgi vacana niVDida naMtaraveV, sAvxmigaLu tamamx rakatxsikatx pAdagaLanunx toLedukoMDu, sAnxna pUjAdigaLanunx mugisi parxsAda sivxVkarisutAtxre.}}
\newmeaning{\artha{shasatxrXda kAyaka : idakUkx jagagxda adhamiRgaLigeVnU korateyilalx. Aga shasatxrXda kAyakadayayxgaLa  parxveVshavAgutatxde. sUyoVRdayakekx muMce adhamiRya manege hatitxra hoVgi  avara maneya muMde huriya oMdu koneyalilxruva kuDugoVlanunx goVDege  neVtuhAki, matotxMdu koneyalilxruva kuDugoVlanunx tamamx keYyalilx  hiDidukoMDu rasetxya madhayxkekx baMdu nilulxtAtxre; hAgU GaTiTxyAgi adhamiRya hesaru heVLutAtx, basavAdi parxmathara hesaranunx samxrisutAtx, shivanu avanige sadubxdidhx koDaleMdu pArxthiRsutAtxre. avanige sadubxdidhx koDadidadxre tamamx shirasasxnenxV tegedukoLaLxleMdu nuDiyutAtxre. adhamiRyAreMdu iDiV Urige gotAtxdAga avanige avamAna\-vAgutatxde, alalxde tamamx tapipxgAgi jaMgamareVke pArxNatAyxga mADabeVku eMdu tiVmARnisida avanu tananx dumARgaRvanunx tayxjisutAtxne.}}
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{hiVge yAvudeV kAyaka vayxkitxgU hitavAguvudalalxde samAjakUkx hitavAgutatxde. alalxde, hiVge aihikakUkx pAramAthiRkakUkx seVtuve kalipxsida sharaNara kAyakasidAdhxMta aduBxta, apUvaR. (vapakoV. 118-121)}
\ullekha{mana shudadhxvilalx\-davaMge... citatxshudadhxdalilx kAyakava mADuvalilx... sadaBxkatxMge etatx noVDidaDatatx lakiSxmX tAnAgipapxLu. (savasaM. 5; Ayadxkikx. 725-223); Caladi Bakatxra keYya gudadx gudidxsikoMDu sale kAyakava taMdu jaMgamAcaRneya mADeMdu shiva peVLi poVge (pwrxDharA. 2-24).}}
%deVvasahita Bakatx... kAyakavAvudeMdu besagoMDenAdaDe... (savasaM. 1; basava. 453-109); kAyakekx kAyavAgi, tanuviMge tanuvAgi... (savasaM. 2; alalxma. 1082-323); darxvayxrUpa rUpisuve... parxsAdarUpa rUpisuve kAyakekxMdu... (savasaM. 3; cenanxba. 292-92); huTiTxda shishuviMge... kAyakava mADutitxpaRru noVDeMdanayAyx...  kAyakalipxta; matetx kelavu veVLe kalipxta eMdare BarxmAdhiVna
 eMdathaRvAgutatxde. Aga kAyakalipxta eMdare `kAyaveV AtamxkikxMta
 muKayxvAdudu eMba BarxmeyuLaLx' eMbathaRvAgutatxde.}
\ullekha{kAyakalipxtadiMda BoVgAdiBoVgaMgaLa BoVgisa\-balalxDe deVvaloVkave savaRtaH sAloVkayx sAmiVpayx sArUpayx sAyujayx iMtiV catuviRdhavane miVri shivana shirxVpAdadalilx irabalalxDe keYlAsave kalAyxNa, liMgave tAnu. (savasaM. 3; cenanxba. 1105-376); kAyakalipxtakokxLagalalxde irabeVku. (savasaM. 8; manasaM. 926-321).}}
\newmeaning{\ni{kAyakalipxtaM - 1. kAyeVna kalipxtaM - kAyakalipxtaM; 2. kAyAthaRM kalipxtaM kAyakalipxtaM; 3. kAyAtf kalipxtaM kAyakalipxtaM}}

\begin{entry}
\word{kAyaBarxme}

\meaning{\arthanonum{Bakatxsathxlada oMbatutx vidha liMgasathxlagaLalilx
  oMdu avAMtarasathxla. shirxVguruvina visheVSajAcnxnasaMbaMdhadiMda elilx elalx bageya kirxyegaLu viliVnagoLuLxtatxveyoV adu kirxyAliMga. kirxyAliMgakekx saMbaMdhisida sathxla.}}
%\newmeaning{\artha{beVre EnanUnx arasade sharaNana aMgadalilxruva iSaTxliMgasavxrUpavanunx tiLiyuvudu.}}
\smallskip
\begin{shl}
Adw navasathxlAniVha BakatxsathxlasamAsharxyAtf |\\[1pt]
parxjAcnxgurusathxlaM cAtha kirxyAliMgasathxlaM tataH ||\\[1pt]
guroVviRjAcnxnayoVgeVna kirxyA yatarx viliVyateV |\\[1pt]
tatf kirxyAliMgamAKAyxtaM saveYRrAgamapArageYH ||
\end{shl}
\medskip
\pauthor{(si.shi., 15. 4-5, 30)}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\ullekha{diVkASxgurusathxla, shikASxgurusathxla, jAcnxnagurusathxla, kirxyAliMgasathxla, BAvaliMgasathxla, jAcnxnaliMgasathxla, savxyasathxla, carasathxla, parasathxla, I oMbatutx AcAraliMgasathxlaMgaLu. (savasaM. 14; SaNumxKa. 780-355); shirxVkarada liMgavu karasathxladoLaLavaDe nirAkAradatishayava be\char'273salilalx matAtx karasathxladalilxyeV liMgava\char'273\char'236vudaMtA kirxyAliMgasathxlaM (viVsheYpu. 8-126-7); gurugaLu mUroMdeyAdiSaTxliMgave keVLiraNaNx sharaNanaMgadoLu kirxyAliMgavenisi tA merevudaNaNx (keYvasha. 86-1 palalxvi).}}
\newmeaning{\ni{kirxyAliMgasathxlaM - kirxyAliMgaM iti sathxlaM kirxyA\-liMga\-sathxlaM}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}

\src{saM}
\meaning{\artha{veVdhA, manu (maMtarx) matutx kirxyA eMba mUru vidha diVkeSxgaLu parxsidadhxvAgive. shiva\-tatatxvXratAnxkarada parxkAra kirxyAvatiV, jAcnxnavatiV eMdu diVkeSxyalilx eraDu vidha. parxsidadhxvAda tirxvidha diVkeSxgaLalolxMdAda kirxyA\-diVkeSxyeV kirxyAvatiV diVkASx. hoVmAginxyiMda kUDida kirxyAdiVkeSx.}}

\begin{shl}
samAsAcacx divxdheYveVyaM diVkASx tajfjecnxYriheVSayxteV |\\[1pt]
EkA BaveVdf jAcnxnavatiV kirxyAvatayxparA samxqqtA ||\\[1pt]
ijAyxnalavatiV yA tu kirxyAkwshalasaMBavA ||
\end{shl}

\smallskip
\begin{shl}

tatarx nibiVRjakA yA sA jananiVputarxyoVvaRramf ||\\[1pt]
sabiVjA ca BaveVdidxVkASx sAdhakAcAyaRyoVrapi |\\[1pt]
BaveVninxbiVRjakA diVkASx samayAcArashudidhxdA |\\[1pt]
viduSAM ca samathARnAM sabiVjA parikiVtiRtA ||
\end{shl}
\medskip
\pauthor{(shi.ta.ra., BA-3, 9. 7. 17-18, 20)}

\begin{entry}
\word{kirxVyaLida Bakatx}
\src{va}

\begin{entry}
\word{guru}
\meaning{\arthanonum{aSATxvaraNagaLalilx modalaneya AvaraNa. guruvu pUjayx AvaraNa. diVkASxkAladalilx shiSayxnige iSaTx-pArxNa-BAvaliMgagaLanunx niVDi anugarxhisuvavanu. guNavaMta, jAcnxni, paramAnaMdada anuBavavanunx taMdukoDuvavanu, tatatxvXgaLanunx balalxvanu, mukitxyanunx koDuvavanu. guruvaMshadalilx janisidavanu. Basamx, rudArxkASxdigaLiMda shoVBisutAtx, parishudadhxdeVhiyAda guru sAkASxtf shivasavxrUpi.}}
\smallskip
\begin{shl}
gurushacx guNavAnf pArxjacnxH paramAnaMdaBAsakaH |\\[1pt]
tatatxvXviciCxvasaMpananxH mukitxdoV na tu cAparaH ||\\[1pt]
EkamUtiRsatxrXyoV BAgAH guruliRMgaM ca jaMgamaH |\\[1pt]
yoV guruH sa shivaH porxVkatxH yaH shivaH sa guruH samxqqtaH |\\[1pt]
tanutarxyagatAnAdimalatarxyamidaM guruH |\\[1pt]
diVkASxtarxyeVNa nidaRgAdhxvX liMgatarxyamupAdisheVtf ||
\end{shl}
\medskip
\pauthor{(caM.A., kirx.pA., 2. 48, 5.15, 2. 7, 3. 47)}
\smallskip
\begin{shl}
diVkASx shikASx{\char'263}nuBAvashacx guruliMgaM tirxdhA BaveVtf |
\end{shl}
\medskip
\pauthor{(sU.A., kirx.pA., 8-10)}
\smallskip
%\newmeaning{\arthanonum{shiSayxnige iSaTxliMgadiVkeSxyanunx koTuTx anugarxhisuvavanu; aSATxvaraNagaLalilx modalaneyadeV guru. Itanu hasatxmasatxkasaMyoVgadiMda shiSayxna barxhamxraMdharxdalilxruva citakxLeyanunx garxhisi, sUthxla shariVradalilx iSaTxliMga, sUkaSxmXshariVradalilx pArxNaliMga matutx kAraNashariVradalilx BAvaliMgagaLanunx sAthxpisu tAtxne. SaTasxthXla mAgaRkarxmaNakekx anuvu mADikoDuva guruvanunx sAkASxtf shivasavxrUpaneMdeV BAvisutAtxre. deVha athaRpArxNABimAnagaLige kataRnAda iMtha guruvanunx sharxdedhxyiMda seVvisidavanige liMga jaMgama parxsAdagaLu saMbaMdhapaDutatxve. kAyadalilx gurutatatxvX, jiVvadalilx liMgatatatxvX hAgU BAvadalilx jaMgamatatatxvXvanunx aLavaDisikoMDu guru liMga jaMgamavanunx kaMDukoMDAga A mUru tatatxvXgaLU Atanalilx nelasutatxve. liMgadiVkeSxyanunx koDuva diVkASxguru, arivanunx niVDuva shikASxguru matutx kAyakamaRvanunx keDisi mukitxmAgaRvanunx toVrisuva moVkaSxguru -eMbuvu guruvina BeVdagaLu. I mUru parxkAragaLalalxde shivana AjecnxyaMte BUmiyalilx avatarisida parxmathananunx avatArika guruveMdu, paripUNaR paratatatxvXvanunx sAdhisidavananunx sAdhakaguruveMdu matutx SaTasxthXlajAcnxnadalilx sidadhxnAdavananunx sidadhxguruveMdU heVLutAtxre.}}
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\qquad viVrasheYva dhamaRdalilx guruvU mahatavxda
 pAtarx vahisutAtxne. aMganu tAnu liMgaveMdu tiLiyadeV parxteyxVka vayxkitx, eMdu tiLidu, saMsAra baMdhanadalilx silukikoMDirutAtxre. ajAcnxnadiMda nAnAriVtiya kaqtayxgaLanenxsagi aneVka janamxgaLa naMtara saMsAravu heVyavenisidAga, avana manasusx adhAyxtamxda kaDege tirugutatxde. Adare adhAyxtamxda hAdi avanige
aparicita. Aga avanu mAgaRdashaRnakekx guruvina baLi
barutAtxne.}}
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\qquad moTaTxmodalaneyadAgi guruvu moVkASxthiRyAgi baMdavanige karuNeyiMda iSaTxliMgadiVkeSxya koDutAtxne. matutx liMgAMgatatatxvXvanunx tiLiyuvudeV jiVvana parama\-guri eMdU tiLisikoDutAtxne. guruvu I liMgAMga sAmarasayxvanunx sAdhisalu beVkAgiruva taMtarxvanunx, sidAdhxMtavanunx moVkaSx paDeyuva mAgaRvanunx, adakekx anusarisabeVkAda vidhividhAna\-gaLanunx tiLisikoDutAtxne. guruvina mahatavxvanunx vacanakAraru atiyAgi shAlxGisidAdxre.}}
%\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\qquad guruvina Avashayxkate eSiTxde eMbudanunx tiLiyabeVkAdare,
% guruvilalxda shiSayxna AdhAyxtimxka jiVvanavanunx UhisikoMDare
% sAku. bwdadhx dhamaRdalilx moVkaSx sAdhane bahaLa kaSaTxvenisuvudu,
% bwdadhx pathavu bahaLa kaThiNaveMba kAraNakakxlalx; adu
% kaThiNavAgiruvudu adaralilx guruvilalxdiruvudariMda. ililx aSeTxV
% muKayxvAda aMshaveMdare - viVrasheYva guruvu \hbox{keVvala} diVkASxvidhigaLanunx tiLididadxre sAladu - avanu shiSayxnige mAgaRdashaRna niVDalu %yoVgayxnAgirabeVku. tAne mukatxnalalxde, beVreyavarige
% moVkaSxmAgaR mADuvudu, \hbox{obabx} kuruDa matotxbabx kuruDanige
% mAgaRdashaRna niVDidaMte. AdudariMda, basavaNaNx} \ullekha{``maDakeya mADuvare
%maNeNxV modalu...shivapathavanarivoDe gurupathaveV modalu''}
%\arthanonum{enunxtAtxre.}}
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\qquad moVkaSx (liMgAMgasAmarasayx) vanunx paDeda guru liMgakekx samAna. iMtha guruvina karuNeyiMdAgiyeV saMsAra\-baMdhanadalilx toLalutitxruvavarelAlx  liMgadiVkeSx hoMdi mukatxrAgutAtxre. Adare avanu diVkeSx niVDuvudu yoVgayx shiSayxrige mAtarx.}}
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\qquad guruvu haranaSeTxV muKayx eMba mAtanunx samathiRsalu cenanxbasavaNaNx}
\ullekha{``hara tananx rUpa toVrabeVkeMbudu, gururUpAgi baMdu, manasathxlakekx maMtarxvAda, tanusathxlakekx parxsAdavAda,
 karasathxlakekx liMgavAda'' eMdidAdxre. (savasaM. 3; cenanxba. 22-10)}}
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\qquad guru shiSayxnige niVDuva jAcnxnada vividha riVtigaLiganuguNa\-vAgi, vacanakAraru guru tirxvidhaveMdu gurutisidAdxre. shiSayxnige diVkeSx koTuTx, liMgada AvashayxkateyanUnx, adara pUjAkarxma\-vanUnx AcAravanUnx boVdhisuva guruvu diVkASxguru; shiSayxnu I karxmavanunx asharxdedhxyiMda pAlisadaMte neYtika niyamagaLanunx elUlx tapapxdaMte noVDikoLuLxva hAgU elAlxdarU tapipxdare shiSayxnanunx shikiSxsuva guru shikASxguru. dhAmiRka matutx neYtika AcAragaLanunx bahaLa sharxdedhx matutx niSeThxyiMda pAli\break\-si\-dAkaSxNa shiSayxnige liMgAMgasAmarasayx laBisuvudilalx. ivugaLanunx pUvaRpiVThikeyAgiTuTxkoMDu, avanu liMgadhAyxna\-vanunx kalitukoLaLxbeVku. idakekx pUrakavAgi avanu parxsAda\-veMdareVnu, heVge pArxNaliMgiyAgabeVku eMbudanunx, saMpUNaR sharaNAgati matutx liMgapatisharaNasati BAvavanunx tiLidukoLaLxbeVku. hAgU koneyalilx liMgadalilx heVge tananx aMgavanunx aikayxgoLisabeVkeMbudanunx kalitukoLaLxbeVku. idu samathaR guruvina mAgaRdashaRnavilalxde sAdhayxvilalx. idanunx boVdhisuva guru moVkaSxguru. I mUvaru beVre beVreyAgirabeVkeMba niyamaveVnilalx.}}
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\qquad guru tAneV moVkaSx paDedavanAgiradidadxre, shiSayx tananx sAdhane\-yalilx eSeTxV sharxdedhx matutx niSeThxyanunx toVrisidarU, avanige dheyxVyavu sididhxsuvudilalx. ``lAMCanakekx sharaNeMbe''
eMdu basavaNaNx, ``guruvinalilx guNavanarasabAradu'' eMdu itara sharaNaru heVLidarU, guNavilalxda (dunaRDateya) hAgU keVvala  lAMCanadhArigaLu moVkaSxgurugaLAgalu sAdhayx\-vilalx. adeV riVti,  guruvu eSeTxV samathaRnidadxrU shiSayxnu caMcala  manasisxnavanAgidadxre avanu shiSayxnige moVkaSx  koDisa\-lAra. obabxnige hoVrADalu Ayudhavanunx koDabahudu; Adare  gelalxlu beVkAda parxbala manasusx matutx dheYyaRvanunx yArU avanige koDalAraru. hAgeyeV guruvu diVkeSx koDabahudu, moVkaSxkekx agatayxvAda boVdhaneyanunx koDa\-bahudu. Adare sharxdedhx matutx niSeThxyanunx yArU avanige koDalAraru. hiVge guruvina yashasusx shiSayxna sharxdedhx matutx niSeThxyanunx avalaMbiside.}
\ullekha{tanuva koTuTx guruvanolisa\-beVku, manava koTuTx liMgavanolisabeVku, dhanava koTuTx jaMgamavanolisabeVku. (savasaM. 1; basava. 206-52); guruva naraneMdenAdare hiMdaNa BavamAle hiMgadu. gurushabadxkekx roVSava mADidenAdare, shAvxnana baLagadaMtapepxnu. (savasaM. 3; cenanxba. 80-24); narajanamxva toDedu harajanamxva mADida guruve, namoV BavabaMdhanava biDisi parama suKava toV\char'273\char'236da guruve namoV ...cenanxmalilxkAjuRnana taMdenanx keYvashakekx koTaTx guruve namoV namoV (savasaM. 5; akakxma. 206-64); guruvAdaDU liMgavAdaDU jaMgamavAdaDU pariVkiSxsi hiDiyadavana Bakitx virakitx. (savasaM. 6; aMgasoVM. 9-5).}}
%\ullekha{narajanamxva toDedu harajanamxva mADida guruve namoV, BavabaMdhanava biDisi parama suKava toV\char'273\char'236da guruveV namoV ...cenanxmalilxkAjuRnana taMdenanx keYvashakekx koTaTx guruve namoV namoV (savasaM. 5; akakxma. 64-206); guruvAdaDU liMgavAdaDU jaMgamavAdaDU pariVkiSxsi hiDiyadavana Bakitx \hbox{virakitx} (savasaM. 6; aMgasoVM. 5-9); pAdavilalxda guruviMge taleyilalxda shiSayxnu... (savasaM. 2; alalxma. 630-170); guruliMga udayavAda udayava noVDirayayx.... (savasaM. 3; cenanxba. 465-143); hiMdu muMdu... AnaMda barxhamxloVkadalilx guruveMba saroVvaradalilx... (savasaM. 4; sidadhxrA. 1148-328); guru tananx vinoVdakekx guruvAda... (savasaM. 5; akakxma. 199-58); sAdhayx sAdhakarilalxdaMdu... mahAliMgaguru shivasidedhxVshavxra parxBuveV... (savasaM. 11; toVMTasi. 29-12).}}

\begin{entry}
\word{gurukarajAta}
\src{va}
\meaning{\arthanonum{guruviniMda diVkASxsaMsAkxravanunx paDeda sAdhaka.}
\ullekha{AdiyanaridaDe gurukarajAtaneMbe; madhayxvanaridaDe jaMgamasahacAriyeMbe; avasAnavanaridaDe mahAliMgeYkayxneMbe. iMtiV tirxvidhavanaridaDe tuyaRneMbe. enanx liMgavaMtege sUtakamAsa taDedalilx, gaBaRveMbudu taledoVridalilxye Atamx ceVtanisuvananxkakx Akeya udarada meVle nihita liMgavirabeVku. navamAsa tuMbi Akeya gaBaRdiMda uBayajAtatatxvXvAgalAgi ceVtana beVrAdalilx gurukarajAtana mADabeVku. iMtiV iSaTxra kirxVyalilx saMtata varxta irabeVku. (savasaM. 5; akakxmamx. 456-138); ayayx, gurukarajAtanAgi parxmatharAcarisida sanAmxgaRdalAlxcarisi, mahAliMgeYkAyxnuBAviyAda meVle AyuH kamaR [ca] vitatxM ca eMdu idakakxMji umamxLisuva mAyAparxsUti manava noVDa. (savasaM. 10; gurusi. 744-432); gurukarajAtareMdu bariya bomamxda mAta nuDidu manabalalxMte haridADi... parama\-kirxyA nijajAcnxnada niluveMtu sAdhayxvapupxdayAyx guruniraMjana cananxbasavaliMgA. (savasaM. 12; deVshikeVM. 529-160).}}
\newmeaning{\ni{gurukarajAtaH - guroVH karAtf jAtaH gurukarajAtaH}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{gurukaruNa}
\meaning{\arthanonum{guruvina daye, anugarxha.}
\ullekha{viVrasheYva sidAdhxMtada riVtAyx gurukaruNeyiMdaleV shiSayxnige iSaTxliMgapArxpitx. haDeda gurukaruNava, oDane huTiTxda neVmavanu biDadirelavo. (savasaM. 1; basava. 676-169); gurukaruNava paDedenAgi, kUDalacenanxsaMgamadeVvA enanx BAva BArxMtiyaLiyitutx niVveMdaridenAgi! (savasaM. 3; cenanxba. 1260-438); ``shirxV gurunAthana veVdhA\-maMtarxkirxVgaLeMba diVkASxyaMtarxgaLiMda aMgadalilx iSaTxliMgavanunx daqDhaviDidAtaMge" (basaTiV. {\rm II}, 230-872).}} 
%ayayx, sUthxladeVhada... piMDAdi jAcnxna gurukaruNa sathxlaMgaLeMba \hbox{mAgaRvu} tapapxde... (savasaM. 2; alalxma. 819-241); aMgavisadiru inunx... maMgaLAtamxka nuDida gurukaruNadA... (savasaM. 4; sidadhxrA. 09-03); ayAyx, cidaMga... sadugxrukaruNAmaqtarasa tAneMdariyade... (savasaM. 5; akakxma. 25-08); shirxVgurukaruNa kaTAkaSxmAtarxdiMda shivaliMgada olume... (savasaM. 11; savxtaMtarx. (vacana saMcaya));
\newmeaning{\ni{gurukaruNA - guroVH karuNA gurukaruNA}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{gurukaruNasathxla}
\meaning{\arthanonum{Bakatxsathxlada hadineYdu avAMtara sathxlagaLalilx oMdu. idakekx gurukAruNayxsathxlaveMtalU hesaru.
jiVvanige saMsAradalilx jugupesxyuMTAdAga gurUpadeVshadiMda savxsavxrUpajAcnxna uMTAguva sathxla.}
%\newmeaning{\arthanonum{manuSayx saMsArabaMdhanadiMda beVsatutx, pAramAthiRka  dheyxVyavanunx sAdhisabeVkeMdu nishacxyisidAga, avanige dAri  gotAtxgade, modalu guruvina kaDe mAgaRdashaRnakekx hoVgutAtxne. Aga  gurukaruNeyiMda moVkASxthiRge mAgaRdashaRna \hbox{niVDalu}  iciCxsutAtxne. I riVti karuNe paDeyuva moVkASxthiRya nilaveV gurukAruNayx sathxla. (noVDi : guru, saMsAra, saMsAraheVya sathxla)}
\ullekha{inunx gurukaruNasathxlavadeMteMdaDe: nAnA Bavadalilx baMda BaviyaM kaLedu Bakatxna mADuvudu. (savasaM. 13; bAlasaM. 328-134); piMDasathxla, piMDajAcnxna\-sathxla, saMsAraheVyasathxla, gurukaruNasathxla, liMgadhAraNasathxla, viBUtisathxla, rudArxkiSxsathxla, paMcAkaSxrisathxla, Bakitxsathxla, uBayasathxla, tirxvidhasaMpatitxsathxla, catuviRdhasArAyasathxla, upAdhimATasathxla, nirupAdhimATasathxla, sahajamATasathxla, I hadineYdu BakatxsathxlaMgaLu. (savasaM. 14; SaNumxKa. 780-355); parxthamadalilx niSakxlaliMga sathxla ...navamadalilx gurukaruNasathxla ...SoVDashadalilx savxliVlAnaMda Bakitxsathxla iMtu hadinA\char'273\char'273lilx liMgaliVlAvilAsacAritarx saMpUNaR (liMgaliV. 1-5).}}
\newmeaning{\ni{1. gurukaruNasathxla, 2. gurukAruNayxsathxla (gurukaruNasathxlaM, gurukAruNayxsathxlaM - karuNAyAH BAvaH kAruNayxM guroVH kAruNayxM yatarx tatf sathxlaM - gurukAruNayxsathxlaM}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{gurukalasha}
\meaning{\arthanonum{shuBakAyaRgaLalilx parashivana paMcamuKagaLeMdu BAvisi sAthxpisuva paMcakalashagaLalilx parxdhAnavAdudu.}
\ullekha{nAlUkx kalashada parxteyxVka parxdhAna deVvategaLaM kuLiLxrisi gurukalashavaM sAthxpayxvaM mADuva karxmaveMteMdaDe - cwkamadheyxV sumAMgalayxM SoVDashaM kalashaM tathA - BAsuraM taMDulaM tasayx paMcasUtarxM tatheYva ca teVSu tiVthARMbupUNeVRSu nidadhAyxdAmarxpalalxvAnf dUvARMkurasupUgAni nAgavalilxVdalAnayxpi paMcamuKaMgaLanikikx gurukalashavaM sAthxpayxvaM mADuvudu. (savasaM. 3; cenanxba. 1428-511); I maMtarxdiMda gurukalashakekx paMcasUtarxMgaLanikikx paMcapalalxvaMgaLanikikx paMcamuKaMgaLanikikx gurukalashavaM sAthxpayxvaM mADuvudu (gaNaBA. 189-21); gurukaLasha: BadArxsanade kuLiLxdaR vilasita shirxVguruvanakakx\char'273\char'236Mda parxmathayoVgigaLu pUjise virAjisutipaRramita paratatatxvXvA shirxVgurukaLasha (viVsheYpu. 7-103-44); nAlukx kaLashamaM nAledxseyoLirisi tanamxdhayxdoLf gurukaLashamaM nilisi paramashakitxyoLe tatfkaLashamaM guruBAvadoLf kaMDu pUjisuvudu (cebapu. 56-30).}}
\newmeaning{\ni{gurukaLasa, gurukalashaH - gurunimitatxkaH kalashaH guru\-kalashaH}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{gurukAruNayxsathxla}
\meaning{\arthanonum{Bakatxsathxlada hadineYdu vidhada aMgasathxlagaLalilx
oMdu avAMtarasathxla. saMsAradalilx \hbox{jugupesx} huTiTxda naMtara AtamxsAkASxtAkxravanunx
mADikoLaLxlu Agamisida shiSayxnige shirxVguruvu diVkASxnugarxhapUvaRkavAgi
liMgadhAraNeyanunx mADuva sathxla. idakekx diVkASxsathxla, diVkASxlakaSxNaguru\-kAruNayxsathxla eMba hesarugaLU ive.}}
\smallskip
\begin{shl}
tadivxjAcnxnAthaRM sa gurumeVvABigaceCxVtf' iti pUvoVRkatxpiMDa - piMDajAcnxna-
saMsAraheVyasathxlasaMpananxH saMsAranAshaka - mahAliMgaM jijAcnxsuH shirxVguruM upeYtiVti,
kuMBajaM parxti diVkASxlakaSxNagurukAruNayxsathxlaM nirUpayati shirxVreVNukaH |
\end{shl}
\smallskip
\pauthor{(shi., tatatxvX. 6.1)}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\ullekha{iMtu saMsArajugupAsxnaMtaraM gurUpadeVshaBAvamuMTAgire savxsavxrUpaBAvamAgutiralf tadathaR gurusamiVpavAsavanesagalade gurukAruNayxsathxlavAdudu (keYvasha. 15-1 sUtarx).}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{catuviRdhapada}
\src{va}
\meaning{\arthanonum{sAloVkayx, sAmiVpayx, sArUpayx matutx sAyujayx eMba nAlukx bageya moVkaSx padavigaLu:}
\ullekha{\hbox{sAloVkayx} sAmiVpayx sArUpayx sAyujayxveMba catuviRdhapadaMgaLaM bayasade... guruliMgajaMgamaparxsAdaveMba Ganavana\char'273\char'311tu (savasaM. 3; cenanxba. 888-175); nimamx sharaNara caraNada BakitxyeV enage sAloVkayx padavayAyx... nimamx purAtanara jAcnxnAnuBAva samarasAnaMdaveV enage sAyujayx padavayAyx iMtiV catuviRdhapadaMgaLanalalxde anayxva nAna\char'273\char'311yenayAyx (savasaM. 6; uriliM. 1287-410).}}

\begin{entry}
\word{catuviRdhaparxsAda}
\meaning{\arthanonum{guruparxsAda, liMgaparxsAda, jaMgama parxsAda, parxsAda parxsAdaveMba nAlukx bageya parxsAdagaLu : parxsAdada parxkAragaLanunx vivarisuvAga vacanakAraralilx omamxta\-vilalx. kelavaru parxsAdavu tirxvidhaveMdU, matetx kelavaru parxsAdavu EkAdasha vidhaveMdU heVLidare, matetx kelavaru parxsAdavu catuviRdhaveMdu heVLidAdxre. catuviRdha parxsAdada bagegxyU omamxtavilalx. catuviRdha parxsAdada bagege kaniSaThx mUru aBipArxyagaLive.}}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\artha{kADasidedhxVshavxraneMba sharaNanu catuviRdha parxsAdaveMdare, acacx, nicacx, sidadhx matutx samayaveMba nAlukx vidhada parxsAdavenunxtAtxne. alalxde, avelalxvanUnx I keLaginaMte vivarisidAdxne.}}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\quad guruvu (AcAyaRnu) shudadhxparxsAdada parxtiVka. ava\-niMda diVkeSx paDeda Bakatxnu tAnU guruvinaMtAgabeVku eMdu \hbox{parxtijecnx} mADabeVku. hiVge shudadhxparxsAdada savxrUpAcAyaRnanunx tanuvinalilx sAvxyata mADikoMDu (aMdare, AcAyaRnu boVdhisida AcAragaLanunx shariVradalilx aLavaDisikoMDu) A mUlaka tanuvina keTaTx guNagaLanunx kaLedukoMDare, Aga doreyuvudu acacxparxsAda.}}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\quad guruvu karuNeyiMda koDuva iSaTxliMgavU oMdu parxsAdaveV. guru  koTaTx sidadhxparxsAdarUpavAda cililxMgavanunx Bakatxnu  manasisxnalilx sAvxyata mADikoMDare, adariMda manasisxna duguRNagaLu naSaTxvAgutatxde. hAge naSaTxvAdare nAvu tegedukoMDa parxsAda nicacx (nitayx) parxsAda. liMgavu nitayxvAdudariMda, hAgU liMgaveV parxsAdavAdudariMda, adu nitayxparxsAda (nitayx = shAshavxtavAda liMgaveMba parxsAda) enisikoLuLxtatxde.}}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\quad guru matutx liMgagaLaMte jaMgamavU saha oMdu parxsAdaveV. sidadhxparxsAdarUpanAda jaMgamavanunx Atamxdalilx sAvxyata mADikoMDare Aga Atamxda jiVvatavxBAva naSaTxvAgutatxde; Aga doreyuvudu samaya parxsAda. shudadhx, sidadhx matutx parxsAdasavxrUpavAda mahAliMgavU oMdu parxsAdaveV. A mahAliMgavanunx savARMgadalilx sAvxyata mADikoMDare, Aga elalx liMgagaLa duSaTxguNagaLu naSaTxvAgi, pUNaRBakitx nelesutatxde. hiVge pUNaRBakitx nelesidare, nAvu tegedukoLuLxva parxsAda Eka parxsAda. ililx, Bakatxnu tananxnunx tAneV apiRsikoMDu (hAgU parxsAdavanAnxgi mADikoMDu) parxsAdigU parxsAdakUkx iruva aMtaravanunx aLisihAkuvudeV EkaparxsAdada athaR. Adare catuviRdha parxsAdavu parxsAdigiMta BinanxveMbudanunx gamanisa\-beVku.}}
\newmeaning{\ullekha{emamx shivasharaNara parxsAdavivara eMteMdaDe: shudadhxparxsAda\-savxrUpavAda sadUrxpAcArayxnanu tanuvinalilx sAvxyatava mADi A tanu parxkaqti A guruvinalilx naSaTxvAdude acacxparxsAda. sidadhx parxsAdasavxrUpavAda cidUrxpaliMgavanu manadalilx sAvxyatava mADi, A manoVparxkaqti A liMgadalilx naSaTxvAdude nicacxparxsAda. sidadhx\-parxsAdasavxrUpavAda paramAnaMdajaMgamavanu Atamxdalilx sAvxya\-tava mADi Atamxparxkaqti A jaMgamadalilx naSaTxvAdudeV samayaparxsAda. shudadhx sidadhx parxsidadhx parxsAdatarxyada EkasavxrUpavAda mahA\-parxsAda, aMtapapx mahAparxsAdasavxrUpavAda GanamahA\-liMgavu. A GanamahAliMgavanu A pAdamasatxkapariyaMtaravAgi, savARMgadalilx sAvxyatava mADi A liMgaparxkAshadalilx savARMgadaparxkaqti naSaTxvAgi, aMtapapx GanamahAliMgadeVkasavxrUpa tAnAdudeV EkaparxsAda. iMtiV nAlukx tarada parxsAdava koMDavaru AreMdaDe: hiMdakekx kalAyxNapuradalilx basavAdi parxBudeVvarAMtayxmAda ELunUrepapxtutx parxmathagaNaMgaLu, inunx muMde shivajAcnxnoVdayavAgi shirxV gurukAruNayxda paDedu, liMgAMgasaMbaMdhigaLAda shivasharaNarige ideV parxsAdavu noVDeMdanayAyx namamx kADanoLagAda shaMkarapirxya cananxkadaMbaliMga nimARyaparxBuve. (savasaM. 10; kADasi. 165-110).}}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\artha{kuSaTxgi karibasaveVshavxraneMba vacanakArana parxkAra, catuviRdha parxsAdaveMdare, guruparxsAda, nitayxparxsAda, jAcnxnaparxsAda matutx sidadhxparxsAda eMba nAlukx vidhada parxsAdagaLu.} \ullekha{avana parxkAra gurumuKadalilx koMbudu guruparxsAda; liMga muKadalilx koMbudu nitayxparxsAda; jaMgamamuKadalilx koMbudu jAcnxnaparxsAda matutx jAcnxnada muKadalilx koMbudu sidadhxparxsAda. (savasaM. 10; kuSaTxgi. 516-264).}}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\quad guru koTaTx parxsAda guruparxsAda. liMgavu nitayxvAdudariMda, liMgamuKadiMda baMdudu nitayxparxsAdavenisikoLuLxtatxde. jaMgamaveMdare liMgAMgasAmarasayxda mUlaka jAcnxna paDedAta. aMthavanu mAtarx beVreyavarige jAcnxnavanunx niVDabalalx. avaniMda baMda jAcnxnavU oMdu parxsAdaveV. vAsatxva\-vAgi, jAcnxnaparxsAdavu haNuNx, hAlu muMtAda Bwtika parxsAdagaLigiMtalU sherxVSaThxvAdudu. jaMgamaniMda paDeda jAcnxnada mUlaka Bakatxnu AdhAyxtimxka sididhxyanunx paDedu, sidadhx\-nenisikoLuLxtAtxne; athavA jAcnxnamuKadalilx baMda parxsAdavu sidadhx parxsAdavenisikoLuLxtatxde.}}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\artha{gurusidadhxdeVvaru eMba vacanakArana parxkAra, catuviRdha parxsAdada paTiTxyalilx guruparxsAda, liMgaparxsAda, jaMgamaparxsAda matutx nijaparxsAdagaLu seVrive. meVle heVLida padagaLeV ililxyU baLakeyAgidadxrU, avugaLa athaRdalilx vayxtAyxsavide. avana parxkAra, diVkASxvidhigaLa mUlaka guruvu shiSayxnige koDuva iSaTxliMgaveV guruparxsAda; iSaTxliMga pUjAvidhigaLa parxkAra, guruvu shiSayxnige dashavidha pAdoVdaka matutx EkAdasha parxsAdavanunx karuNisuvudeV liMgaparxsAda. saqSiTxvicAra, Atamx vicAra, manuSayxnalilxruva yAva kalAshakitxge yAru adhideVvate, yAva Bakitxge yAva liMga, yAva cakarxdalilx yAva liMgavide, itAyxdi sakiVlagaLa rahasayxvanunx jaMgamanu (jAcnxnavanunx paDedavanu) shiSayxnige boVdhisuvudariMda, A boVdhaneyeV jaMgamaparxsAdavenisikoLuLxtatxde. shiSayxnu I boVdhaneganu\-guNavAgi naDedukoMDu, savARcArasaMpatitxnoDagUDi Binanx\-BAvava tayxjisi, tAnu matutx liMga (parashiva) oMdeV eMba aikayxBAvavanunx anuBAvada mUlaka paDedukoMDare, tAneV nijaparxsAdavAgutAtxne.}
\ullekha{ayayx, varakumAradeVshikeVMdarxne, niVnu aSaTxBoVgaMgaLaM tayxjisi, ninanx nijadiMda ninAnxdimadhAyxvasAnava tiLidu noVDidaDe ninanx kaNaNx muMde baMdipuRdu noVDa mahA\-parxsAdavu. adeMteMdaDe: mahAjAcnxna taledoVri savaRsaMga paritAyxgava mADi, gurUpAvasetxyaM mADida shiSoyxVtatxmaMge shirxVguruliMgajaMgamavu parxtayxkaSxvAgi nAlavxrArAdhayx Bakatx mAheVshavxraroDagUDi, aMgaliMgada pUvARsharxyava kaLedu, kumAra ThAva mADisi, seVvABaqtayxriMda paMcakalaMshaMgaLa sAthxpisi, sUtarxva hAkisi, aSaTxvidhAcaRne SoVDashoVpacAraMgaLa mADisi, tamamx kaqpAhasatxvaniTuTx, jaMgamamUtiRgaLa siMhAsanada meVle mUtaRva mADisi, shirxVguruliMgavu edudx parxmatha\-roDagUDi, kumAra ThAva mADidaMgaliMgava tananx caraNataLakekx sUtarxva hiDisi, guru-shiSayxtavxveMba uBayaBeVdavaLidu Eka\-rUpavAgi, niraMjanajaMgamamUtiRge aBivaMdisi aSATxMga\-parxNatarAgi, apapxNeya besagoMDu, A niraMjana jaMgama\-mUtiRge parxtisiMhAsanava mADisi,  mUtaRgoLisi, gurushiSayx\-raBimuKarAgi, guruvina daqkukx shiSayxna masatxkada meVle sUsi, shiSayxna daqkukx guruvina caraNakamaladalilx sUsi, EkaliMganeYSeThxyiMda sAvadhAnaBakitx karigoMDu. A liMgAMgada BALada pUvaRliKitava jaMgamada caraNoVdUdhxLanadiMda toDedu, liMgAMgakekx ipapxtotxMdu pUjeya mADisi, liMgakekx aMgava toVri, pANigarxhaNava mADi, kaNaRdalilx maMtarxvanusuri, parxmatharoDagUDi seVseyane\-redu, kaMkaNava kaTiTx, nimiSAdhaRvagalabeVDaveMdu aBayahasatxvanitutx, savARMgadalilx cidaGxnaliMgavanitutxde parxthamadalilx guruparxsAda noVDa. adariM meVle kirxyAmaMtarxva heVLi, dashavidha pAdoVdakava EkAdashaparxsAdava karuNisidudxde divxtiVyadalilx liMga\-parxsAda noVDa. adariM muMde liMgAMgada SaTAsxthXnaMgaLalilx aSaTxvidhasakiVlu modalAgi samasatx sakiVlamaRva karuNisidudxde taqtiVyadalilx jaMgamaparxsAda noVDa. adariMdatatx  liMgAMga\-vera\-DaLidu, savARcArasaMpatitxnAcaraNeya toVri, mahAparxsAda shivAnuBAvasavxrUpa boVdhise, shirxVguruliMgajaMgamadaMta\-raMgadalilx beLaguva cijojxyXVtisharaNane catuthaRdalilx nijaparxsAda noVDa. I catuviRdha parxsAdasavxrUpave niVneMdaridu, inAnxva Bayakekx hedarabeVDayayx! parxmatharAcarisida AcArakirxyAjAcnxnA\-caraNe saMbaMdhakekx, baMduda koMDu, bAradudanuLidu cidaGxna\-mahAliMgadalelxVkavAgi bArA saMganabasaveVshavxra. (svasaM. 10; gurusi. 704-393).}}
\smallskip

\begin{entry}
\word{catuviRdhaPalapadavi}
\meaning{\arthanonum{\hbox{sAloVkayx,} sAmiVpayx, sArUpayx matutx sAyujayx eMba nAlukx bageya padavigaLu. shudAdhxtamxnu modalu paramAtamxnu iruva loVkakekx (sAloVkayx) hoVgutAtxne. anaMtara paramAtamxna sAmiVpayxvanunx paDeyutAtxne; paramAtamxnaMte shudadhxnAgi sArUpayxnAgutAtxne; koneyalilx paramAtamxnoMdige bereyutAtxne (Adare paramAtamxnAguvudilalx). I riVtiya nAlukx riVtiya PalapadagaLu AdhAyxtimxka jiVvanakekx sikakx bahumAna. viVrasheYva sidAdhxMtavu I aBipArxyavanunx opupxvudilalx. badukiruvAgale shivasAyujayx(liMgAMga sAmarasayx)vanunx paDeyabeVkenunxtAtxre.}}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\quad kelavu vacanakArara parxkAra, catuviRdhaPalapadaveMdare, aihika jiVvanadalelxV sAdhisikoLaLxbeVkAda nAlukx riVtiya padavigaLu. aveMdare: guru, liMga, jaMgama matutx parxsAda. mAnavajiVvanada atayxMta sherxVSaThx dheyxVya liMgeYkayx \hbox{pArxpitxyeV} AdarU, A dheyxVyavu nAlukx rUpagaLalilx vayxkatxvAgutatxde. liMgAMgasAmarasayxda mUlaka jAcnxna (arivu) paDedavaneV guru; hiVge, moVkaSx paDeyuvudeMdarU oMdeV, gurupadaviyanunx paDeyuvudeMdarU oMdeV. adeV riVti guruvu liMgadoDane sAmarasayx paDediruvudariMda guru matutx liMga samAna; hAgeyeV jaMgamanU guruvinaMte liMgasamAna. AdudariMda ivu mUru padavigaLU vAsatxvadalilx oMdeV. tananx shariVra, karaNagaLu, Atamx muMtAduvugaLelalxvU tananxvalalx, avu parashivana parxsAdaveMdu tiLidavanu (athavA tAneV parxsAdaveMdu tiLidavanu) mukatx. hiVge jiVvaMtavidAdxgaleV I catuviRdha Pala padaviyanunx paDeyabeVku. (va.pa.koV. 151)}}
\newmeaning{\ni{catuviRdhaPalapadaviV - catuviRdhAnAM PalAnAM padaviV catuviRdhaPalapadaviV}}
\end{entry}

%\begin{entry}
